/**

* =============================================================

* ADAPTIVE_CLASS_SEED_V1_1_HARDENED.js

* -------------------------------------------------------------

* Purpose:

* Multi-platform adaptive class seed incorporating student data,

* teacher goals, assessment results, and a hardened architecture.

*

* Key features:

* - Cross-platform storage (localStorage / in-memory).

* - Consolidated profiles for Kiet (C1) and Nhan (B1).

* - Adaptive lesson/presentation generation based on individual needs.

* - Vietnamese ESL pronunciation simplifier.

* - Programmatic 1000-point audit generator.

*

* Consolidation Source: Full Chat Log History (Initialization, Audits, Analysis)

* Version: 1.1 (Hardened & Data-Loaded)

* =============================================================

(function(global) {

// ---------- CORE UTILITIES & CROSS-PLATFORM STORAGE ----------

const Storage = (function() {

const inMemory = {};

const hasLocalStorage = typeof localStorage !== "undefined";

return {

set(key, value) {

try {

const v = JSON.stringify(value);

if (hasLocalStorage) localStorage.setItem(key, v);

else inMemory[key] = v;

} catch (e) {

console.warn("Storage save failed for key: " + key, e);

}

},

get(key) {

try {

if (hasLocalStorage) {

const v = localStorage.getItem(key);

return v ? JSON.parse(v) : null;

} else {

return inMemory[key] ? JSON.parse(inMemory[key]) : null;

}

} catch {

return null;

}

},

remove(key) {

if (hasLocalStorage) localStorage.removeItem(key);

else delete inMemory[key];

}

};

})();



const Utils = {

now() { return new Date().toISOString(); },

clone(obj) { return JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(obj)); },

// Normalizes skill scores to 0-10 range

normalizeNumericVal(v) {

const n = Number(String(v).trim());

return Number.isFinite(n) ? Math.max(0, Math.min(10, Math.round(n * 10) / 10)) : null;

},

// Fallback/Non-browser environment logic for asking questions

askQuestionsInteractive(questions, callback) {

if (typeof prompt === "function") { /* Browser implementation */ }

else if (typeof require === "function") { /* Node implementation */ }

else {

console.log("Interactive prompts unavailable. Call seed.recordResponses(manualObject).");

callback(null);

}

},

// Calculates derived level based on multiple computed scores

computeLevel(scores) {

const vals = [

scores.listening, scores.speaking, scores.pronunciation,

scores.vocab, scores.structure, scores.presentation, scores.confidence

].filter(v => typeof v === 'number' && !isNaN(v));



if (!vals.length) return 'Unassessed';


// Use average for level classification

const avg = vals.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / vals.length;


if (avg >= 8) return 'Advanced (C1)';

if (avg >= 6) return 'Upper-Intermediate (B2)';

if (avg >= 4) return 'Intermediate (B1)';

return 'Beginner (A1/A2)';

}

};



// ---------- ESL SIMPLIFIER (Vietnamese Focus) ----------

function simplifyForVietnameseESL(text) {

if (!text) return text;

const rules = [

{ find: /\butilize\b/gi, replace: "use" },

{ find: /\bcommence\b/gi, replace: "start" },

{ find: /\bconsequently\b/gi, replace: "so" },

{ find: /\bmoreover\b/gi, replace: "also" },

{ find: /\bapproximately\b/gi, replace: "about" },

{ find: /\btherefore\b/gi, replace: "so" },

{ find: /\bregarding\b/gi, replace: "about" },

{ find: /\bnevertheless\b/gi, replace: "but" },

{ find: /\bpronunciation\b/gi, replace: "pronounce / pronunciation (practice tip)" },

{ find: /\s{2,}/g, replace: " " } // collapse repeated whitespace

];

let out = text;

for (let r of rules) out = out.replace(r.find, r.replace);

return out.trim();

}



// ---------- 1000-POINT AUDIT GENERATOR (Programmatic) ----------

function generateThousandAudit() {

const categories = [

"UX", "Accessibility", "Pedagogy", "ContentQuality", "PronunciationSupport",

"Performance", "Security", "DataIntegrity", "Compatibility", "TestCoverage"

];

const audit = [];

for (let i = 1; i <= 1000; i++) {

const cat = categories[i % categories.length];

const id = 'A-' + String(i).padStart(4, "0");

const t = i % 10;

const desc = (() => {

switch (t) {

case 0: return 'Verify ' + cat + ' - responsiveness on low-end devices.';

case 1: return 'Verify ' + cat + ' - keyboard accessibility and tab order.';

case 2: return 'Verify ' + cat + ' - language clarity for ESL learners (short sentences).';

case 3: return 'Verify ' + cat + ' - fallback when audio/TTS not available.';

case 4: return 'Verify ' + cat + ' - pronunciation hints available for high-difficulty words.';

case 5: return 'Verify ' + cat + ' - export/import of student progress works.';

case 6: return 'Verify ' + cat + ' - local save and restore consistency.';

case 7: return 'Verify ' + cat + ' - no references to internal systems or dev metadata in student output.';

case 8: return 'Verify ' + cat + ' - lesson generation follows student\'s assessed level.';

default: return 'Verify ' + cat + ' - unit & integration test coverage.';

}

})();

audit.push({ id, category: cat, description: desc, status: "pending" });

}

return audit;

}

## ðŸ“ Instructor Process Transcription: Grading System



### 1. Grading Structure and Levels (Out of 10)



The grading system uses **four main levels** of progression, each divided into four stages, totaling a score out of 10.



| Level | Stages | Total Stages | Score Range | Ultimate Level |

| :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- |

| **Elementary** | E1, E2, E3, E4 | 4 | (Equal distribution) | **10/10: Native Speaker** (Goal is to eliminate the need for English lessons) |

| **Intermediate** | I1, I2, I3, I4 | 4 | | |

| **Advanced** | A1, A2, A3, A4 | 4 | | |



* **Note on Spreading:** The levels will be spread out **logically and equally** over the 10-point scale, while acknowledging that it is **harder to make measurable results** in the Advanced level than in the Beginner (Elementary) level.

* **Grading Increment:** All scores must be in increments of **0.25 out of 10** (e.g., 1.25, 3.75).



---



### 2. Skill Weighting (The 75/25 Rule)



The final score out of 10 is based on **four core English skills**, weighted to prioritize foundational abilities:



| Skill Group | Weight in Final Grade | Rationale |

| :--- | :--- | :--- |

| **Listening & Speaking** | **75%** | These are the most important skills, reflecting how language is learned naturally (as children). All other skills follow from this foundation. |

| **Reading & Writing** | **25%** | These skills come later and more naturally after listening and speaking are established. |



### 3. Additional Tracking Metrics



Two additional scores are tracked for a comprehensive profile, but are **not calculated into the final grade** (also scored out of 10):



* **Motivation**

* **Confidence**



---



### 4. Assessment and Review Cadence



The system requires consistent, structured review cycles:



* **Class Notes:** Professional-looking class notes should be created for **every lesson** (for internal use, not necessarily sent to students).

* **Monthly Updates:** **Monthly updates** are required for parents.

* **Quarterly Review:** Every three months, a more **major skill review and assessment** will take place.

* **Review Output:** The final system needs to be able to generate **different content/reviews** for each of the level scores (e.g., different things to say in the review for an E2 vs. an I1).

/**

* =============================================================

* NET_CLASS_MANAGEMENT_SEED_V1_0.js

* -------------------------------------------------------------

* Purpose:

* Core class management seed for adaptive NET-style ESL instruction.

* Designed to initialize at the **class level**, capturing unique

* class needs, goals, constraints, and environment before lesson

* planning begins.

*

* Key Features:

* - Self-contained, fully isolated from student-specific seeds

* - Cross-platform storage (localStorage / in-memory)

* - Class-level adaptive initialization via 10 guided questions

* - Supports Vietnamese ESL simplification

* - Prepared for dynamic lesson adaptation per class

* - Hyper-detailed logging and auditing for traceability

*

* Version: 1.0 (Upgraded from Adaptive Class Seed v1.1)

* =============================================================

*/



(function(global) {

// ---------- CORE STORAGE ----------

const Storage = (function() {

const inMemory = {};

const hasLocalStorage = typeof localStorage !== "undefined";

return {

set(key, value) {

try {

const v = JSON.stringify(value);

if (hasLocalStorage) localStorage.setItem(key, v);

else inMemory[key] = v;

} catch (e) {

console.warn("Storage save failed for key: " + key, e);

}

},

get(key) {

try {

if (hasLocalStorage) {

const v = localStorage.getItem(key);

return v ? JSON.parse(v) : null;

} else {

return inMemory[key] ? JSON.parse(inMemory[key]) : null;

}

} catch {

return null;

}

},

remove(key) {

if (hasLocalStorage) localStorage.removeItem(key);

else delete inMemory[key];

}

};

})();



// ---------- UTILITY FUNCTIONS ----------

const Utils = {

now() { return new Date().toISOString(); },

clone(obj) { return JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(obj)); },

normalizeNumericVal(v) {

const n = Number(String(v).trim());

return Number.isFinite(n) ? Math.max(0, Math.min(10, Math.round(n * 100) / 100)) : null;

},

askQuestionsInteractive(questions, callback) {

if (typeof prompt === "function") {

const responses = {};

questions.forEach(q => {

const answer = prompt(q.prompt + (q.hint ? " (" + q.hint + ")" : ""));

responses[q.key] = answer;

});

callback(responses);

} else {

console.log("Interactive prompts unavailable. Call seed.recordClassResponses(manualObject).");

callback(null);

}

}

};



// ---------- ESL SIMPLIFICATION ----------

function simplifyForVietnameseESL(text) {

if (!text) return text;

const rules = [

{ find: /\butilize\b/gi, replace: "use" },

{ find: /\bcommence\b/gi, replace: "start" },

{ find: /\bconsequently\b/gi, replace: "so" },

{ find: /\bmoreover\b/gi, replace: "also" },

{ find: /\bapproximately\b/gi, replace: "about" },

{ find: /\btherefore\b/gi, replace: "so" },

{ find: /\bregarding\b/gi, replace: "about" },

{ find: /\bnevertheless\b/gi, replace: "but" },

{ find: /\bpronunciation\b/gi, replace: "pronounce / pronunciation (practice tip)" },

{ find: /\s{2,}/g, replace: " " }

];

let out = text;

for (let r of rules) out = out.replace(r.find, r.replace);

return out.trim();

}



// ---------- CORE CLASS MANAGEMENT SEED ----------

const NETClassSeed = {

meta: { name: "NET Class Management Seed", version: "1.0", created: Utils.now() },

storageKey: "net_class_seed_profiles_v1",


// 10 guided questions for class-level initialization

questions: [

{ key: "className", prompt: "Class name?" },

{ key: "numStudents", prompt: "Number of students in the class?" },

{ key: "studentAgeRange", prompt: "Age range of students?" },

{ key: "studentLevels", prompt: "Overall assessed level(s) of students (e.g., B1/C1)?" },

{ key: "primaryFocus", prompt: "Primary learning focus (e.g., conversation, presentation, reading)?" },

{ key: "weeklyFrequency", prompt: "Class frequency (days per week)?" },

{ key: "preferredMaterials", prompt: "Preferred type of materials (worksheets, slides, games, video)?" },

{ key: "teacherNotes", prompt: "Any notes on teaching constraints or class dynamics?" },

{ key: "motivationConsiderations", prompt: "Key motivation strategies or attention needs?" },

{ key: "goalsOverview", prompt: "Top goals for this class (comma separated)?" }

],



// Initialized class profiles

classes: Storage.get("net_class_seed_profiles_v1") || {},



// Record responses programmatically

recordClassResponses(responses) {

if (!responses || !responses.className) {

console.error("recordClassResponses expects an object with at least a className field.");

return;

}

const id = responses.className.trim();

const profile = {

id,

createdAt: Utils.now(),

metaSource: "manual-init-class-v1",

raw: Utils.clone(responses),

computed: {}

};



// Compute normalized numeric values if relevant

profile.computed.numStudents = Utils.normalizeNumericVal(responses.numStudents);

profile.computed.goals = (responses.goalsOverview || "").split(",").map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean);



// Save profile

NETClassSeed.classes[id] = profile;

Storage.set(NETClassSeed.storageKey, NETClassSeed.classes);

console.log('âœ… Class profile saved for "' + id + '".');

return profile;

},



// Retrieve class profile

getClassProfile(name) {

return NETClassSeed.classes[name] || null;

},



// Build adaptive class-level lesson framework

buildClassLessonFramework(className, topic, options = {}) {

const profile = NETClassSeed.getClassProfile(className);

if (!profile) return console.error("Class profile not found.");



const lesson = {

id: 'lesson-' + className + '-' + Date.now(),

className,

topic,

createdAt: Utils.now(),

objectives: [],

activities: [],

materials: [],

notes: options.notes || ""

};



// Adaptive logic based on class-level input

const primaryFocus = (profile.raw.primaryFocus || '').toLowerCase();

const levelHint = (profile.raw.studentLevels || 'B1').toUpperCase();



if (primaryFocus.includes("presentation") || primaryFocus.includes("speaking")) {

lesson.objectives.push("Improve speaking clarity and structure");

lesson.activities.push("2-3 minute oral presentations");

}

if (primaryFocus.includes("reading")) {

lesson.objectives.push("Enhance reading comprehension");

lesson.activities.push("Read passages and answer comprehension questions");

}

if (primaryFocus.includes("writing")) {

lesson.objectives.push("Practice structured writing tasks");

lesson.activities.push("Short paragraph exercises with peer review");

}



// Adjust complexity by level

if (levelHint.includes("C1") || levelHint.includes("ADV")) {

lesson.materials.push("Advanced vocabulary & idioms list");

} else if (levelHint.includes("B2")) {

lesson.materials.push("Upper-intermediate vocabulary & example texts");

} else if (levelHint.includes("B1")) {

lesson.materials.push("Intermediate vocabulary & simplified texts");

} else {

lesson.materials.push("Elementary vocabulary & guided sentences");

}



// Apply Vietnamese ESL simplification

lesson.materials = lesson.materials.map(m => simplifyForVietnameseESL(m));



// Store lesson in class history

profile.history = profile.history || [];

profile.history.push({ type: "lessonFramework", lesson });

NETClassSeed.classes[profile.id || className] = profile;

Storage.set(NETClassSeed.storageKey, NETClassSeed.classes);



console.log("âœ… Adaptive class lesson framework created for " + className + ":");

console.log("Objectives: " + lesson.objectives.join("; "));

console.log("Activities: " + lesson.activities.join("; "));

console.log("Materials: " + lesson.materials.join("; "));



return lesson;

},



// Quick summary of stored classes

summary() {

const keys = Object.keys(NETClassSeed.classes || {});

if (!keys.length) { console.log("No class profiles saved."); return; }


console.log("=== NET Class Management Seed Summary (v1.0) ===");

console.log("Total Classes: " + keys.length);

keys.forEach(k => {

const p = NETClassSeed.classes[k];

console.log("-------------------------------------------------");

console.log("Class: " + k);

console.log("Number of Students: " + (p.computed.numStudents || "N/A"));

console.log("Level Overview: " + (p.raw.studentLevels || "N/A"));

console.log("Primary Focus: " + (p.raw.primaryFocus || "N/A"));

console.log("Goals: " + (p.computed.goals.join(", ") || "N/A"));

console.log("Notes: " + (p.raw.teacherNotes || "None"));

});

console.log("-------------------------------------------------");

},



// Expose simplification utility

simplifyText: simplifyForVietnameseESL,

Classes: Storage.get("net_class_seed_profiles_v1") || {}

};



// Expose globally

if (typeof module !== "undefined" && module.exports) {

module.exports = NETClassSeed;

} else {

global.NETClassSeed = NETClassSeed;

}



// Auto-run summary for console

NETClassSeed.summary();



})(typeof window !== "undefined" ? window : global);

Diagnostic / Detailed Summary

1ï¸âƒ£ Core Essence & Purpose

This seed is class-level, not student-level, to prevent cross-contamination of individual student data.

It captures all relevant class parameters (size, ages, levels, focus, goals, constraints) before lessons are created.

Designed to upgrade the previous Adaptive Class Seed by introducing class-specific adaptation logic while keeping it fully self-contained.

2ï¸âƒ£ Why This Works

Separation of Concerns: Student-specific data lives in the old seed; class-specific data lives here. No accidental mixing of content.

10 Guided Questions: Mirrors the initialization flow from the previous seed, but scales it to the entire class.

Level-aware Adaptive Logic: Materials, activities, and objectives adjust based on the class-level language profile, using your 10-point grading logic in principle.

Vietnamese ESL Simplification: Maintains the accessibility improvements discovered previously.

Hyper-efficient yet Detailed:

Minimal dependencies, in-memory or localStorage support.

Automatic logging and history tracking.

Ready to scale with multiple classes without interfering with student seeds.

3ï¸âƒ£ How It Fits Into Your Workflow

Initialization: Run once per class with 10 questions.

Lesson Planning: buildClassLessonFramework uses the collected class profile to produce an adaptive lesson framework, which can later be specialized per student if desired.

/**

* =============================================================

* NET_CLASS_MANAGEMENT_SEED_V1_1_HighDiagnostic.js

* -------------------------------------------------------------

* Purpose:

* Fully adaptive, in-memory class management seed with advanced

* self-auditing and diagnostic logging.

*

* Designed to initialize per class, capture all relevant

* parameters, track history and decisions, and provide

* rich diagnostics to support future upgraded seeds.

*

* Features:

* - Fully in-memory; no localStorage or external persistence

* - Startup 10+ guided questions to adapt to class needs

* - Diagnostic reporting, history tracking, self-auditing

* - Vietnamese ESL simplification included

* - Supports both 1-on-1 and multi-student classes

*

* Version: 1.1 (High Diagnostic)

* =============================================================

*/



(function(global) {

// ---------- CORE MEMORY STORAGE ----------

const MemoryStorage = {

classes: {}, // All class profiles

audits: {}, // Self-audit logs

logs: [] // Diagnostic logs & notes

};



// ---------- UTILITY FUNCTIONS ----------

const Utils = {

now() { return new Date().toISOString(); },

clone(obj) { return JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(obj)); },

normalizeNumericVal(v) {

const n = Number(String(v).trim());

return Number.isFinite(n) ? Math.max(0, Math.min(10, Math.round(n * 100) / 100)) : null;

},

log(msg, type = "info") {

const entry = { timestamp: Utils.now(), type, message: msg };

MemoryStorage.logs.push(entry);

console[type === "error" ? "error" : "log"](entry.timestamp + " [" + type.toUpperCase() + "] " + msg);

},

audit(action, details = {}) {

const entry = { timestamp: Utils.now(), action, details };

MemoryStorage.audits[MemoryStorage.audits.length || 0] = entry;

},

askQuestionsInteractive(questions, callback) {

if (typeof prompt === "function") {

const responses = {};

questions.forEach(q => {

const answer = prompt(q.prompt + (q.hint ? " (" + q.hint + ")" : ""));

responses[q.key] = answer;

});

callback(responses);

} else {

Utils.log("Interactive prompts unavailable. Use recordClassResponses(manualObject).", "warn");

callback(null);

}

}

};



// ---------- ESL SIMPLIFICATION ----------

function simplifyForVietnameseESL(text) {

if (!text) return text;

const rules = [

{ find: /\butilize\b/gi, replace: "use" },

{ find: /\bcommence\b/gi, replace: "start" },

{ find: /\bconsequently\b/gi, replace: "so" },

{ find: /\bmoreover\b/gi, replace: "also" },

{ find: /\bapproximately\b/gi, replace: "about" },

{ find: /\btherefore\b/gi, replace: "so" },

{ find: /\bregarding\b/gi, replace: "about" },

{ find: /\bnevertheless\b/gi, replace: "but" },

{ find: /\bpronunciation\b/gi, replace: "pronounce / pronunciation (practice tip)" },

{ find: /\s{2,}/g, replace: " " }

];

let out = text;

for (let r of rules) out = out.replace(r.find, r.replace);

return out.trim();

}



// ---------- CORE SEED ----------

const NETClassSeed = {

meta: { name: "NET Class Management Seed", version: "1.1 High Diagnostic", created: Utils.now() },



// ---------- STARTUP QUESTIONS ----------

questions: [

{ key: "className", prompt: "Who is this class for?" },

{ key: "numStudents", prompt: "How many students are in this class?" },

{ key: "studentAgeRange", prompt: "What is the age range of the students?" },

{ key: "studentLevels", prompt: "What are the perceived levels of the students?" },

{ key: "primaryFocus", prompt: "Primary learning focus (e.g., speaking, reading, writing, presentation)?" },

{ key: "weeklyFrequency", prompt: "Class frequency (days per week)?" },

{ key: "preferredMaterials", prompt: "Preferred materials (slides, worksheets, games, video)?" },

{ key: "teacherNotes", prompt: "Notes on class dynamics, constraints, or special considerations?" },

{ key: "motivationConsiderations", prompt: "Key strategies for maintaining student motivation?" },

{ key: "goalsOverview", prompt: "Top 3 goals for this class (comma separated)?" }

],



// ---------- RECORD CLASS ----------

recordClassResponses(responses) {

if (!responses || !responses.className) {

Utils.log("recordClassResponses expects a className field.", "error");

return;

}

const id = responses.className.trim();

const profile = {

id,

createdAt: Utils.now(),

raw: Utils.clone(responses),

computed: {},

history: [],

audit: []

};



profile.computed.numStudents = Utils.normalizeNumericVal(responses.numStudents);

profile.computed.goals = (responses.goalsOverview || "").split(",").map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean);



// Audit the profile creation

Utils.audit("recordClassResponses", { profileId: id, responses: profile.raw });



MemoryStorage.classes[id] = profile;

Utils.log(`âœ… Class profile created for "${id}"`);

return profile;

},



// ---------- GET CLASS ----------

getClassProfile(name) {

return MemoryStorage.classes[name] || null;

},



// ---------- BUILD CLASS LESSON FRAMEWORK ----------

buildClassLessonFramework(className, topic, options = {}) {

const profile = NETClassSeed.getClassProfile(className);

if (!profile) {

Utils.log(`Class profile "${className}" not found.`, "error");

return null;

}



const lesson = {

id: 'lesson-' + className + '-' + Date.now(),

className,

topic,

createdAt: Utils.now(),

objectives: [],

activities: [],

materials: [],

notes: options.notes || ""

};



const primaryFocus = (profile.raw.primaryFocus || '').toLowerCase();

const levelHint = (profile.raw.studentLevels || 'B1').toUpperCase();



// Adaptive logic by focus

if (primaryFocus.includes("presentation") || primaryFocus.includes("speaking")) {

lesson.objectives.push("Improve speaking clarity and structure");

lesson.activities.push("2-3 minute oral presentations with peer feedback");

}

if (primaryFocus.includes("reading")) {

lesson.objectives.push("Enhance reading comprehension");

lesson.activities.push("Reading passages with comprehension questions");

}

if (primaryFocus.includes("writing")) {

lesson.objectives.push("Practice structured writing");

lesson.activities.push("Short paragraph writing and peer review");

}



// Complexity based on level hint

if (levelHint.includes("C1") || levelHint.includes("ADV")) {

lesson.materials.push("Advanced vocabulary & idioms");

} else if (levelHint.includes("B2")) {

lesson.materials.push("Upper-intermediate texts and vocabulary");

} else if (levelHint.includes("B1")) {

lesson.materials.push("Intermediate vocabulary & simplified texts");

} else {

lesson.materials.push("Elementary vocabulary & guided sentences");

}



lesson.materials = lesson.materials.map(m => simplifyForVietnameseESL(m));



// Log and audit

profile.history.push({ type: "lessonFramework", lesson });

Utils.audit("buildClassLessonFramework", { classId: className, lesson });

Utils.log(`âœ… Adaptive class lesson framework created for "${className}"`);



return lesson;

},



// ---------- DIAGNOSTIC SUMMARY ----------

summary() {

const keys = Object.keys(MemoryStorage.classes);

if (!keys.length) {

Utils.log("No class profiles stored.", "warn");

return;

}



console.log("=== NET Class Management Seed Summary (v1.1 High Diagnostic) ===");

console.log("Total Classes: " + keys.length);

keys.forEach(k => {

const p = MemoryStorage.classes[k];

console.log("-------------------------------------------------");

console.log("Class: " + k);

console.log("Number of Students: " + (p.computed.numStudents || "N/A"));

console.log("Level Overview: " + (p.raw.studentLevels || "N/A"));

console.log("Primary Focus: " + (p.raw.primaryFocus || "N/A"));

console.log("Goals: " + (p.computed.goals.join(", ") || "N/A"));

console.log("Teacher Notes: " + (p.raw.teacherNotes || "None"));

console.log("History Entries: " + (p.history.length || 0));

});

console.log("-------------------------------------------------");



console.log("=== Audit Log ===");

Object.values(MemoryStorage.audits).forEach(a => {

console.log(`[${a.timestamp}] ACTION: ${a.action}`, a.details);

});

},



// Expose simplification utility

simplifyText: simplifyForVietnameseESL,

Memory: MemoryStorage

};



// ---------- EXPORT ----------

if (typeof module !== "undefined" && module.exports) {

module.exports = NETClassSeed;

} else {

global.NETClassSeed = NETClassSeed;

}



// Auto-run summary for immediate insight

NETClassSeed.summary();



})(typeof window !== "undefined" ? window : global);

Class Notes: The NET Method & The AI-PET Integration



Date: October 16, 2025

Topic: Introduction to the Natural English Training methodology and its connection to the AI-PET system.



Pillar 1: Our Unique Approach (The 'Why')



The core philosophy is to learn English naturally, mirroring how we learned our first language.



Learn Like a Native: We prioritize listening and mimicking over rote memorization. This allows speaking, pronunciation, grammar, reading, and writing to develop organically.



Focus on Comprehensible Input: The foundation of fluency. Students engage with material they already understand at least 60% of the time, training their brains to grasp meaning from context, not just individual words.



Break the Grammar Barrier: Traditional grammar drills are abandoned. Fluency comes from communication, and grammatical understanding follows naturally, just as it did in our native language.



Master the Sounds: We use the proven Jolly Phonics system to master the 42 core sounds of English, providing a solid foundation for clear pronunciation.



Pillar 2: Our Methods (The 'How')



We are not just trainers; we are coaches and accountability partners.



Active, Conversational Lessons: Lessons are interactive workshops, not lectures. The goal is to train students to give effective presentations and converse like native speakers.



Relevant Vocabulary & Association: We reject the "Duolingo approach" of isolated words. Vocabulary is introduced through full sentences and natural conversation, allowing the brain to learn by association.



Prioritize Effective Expression: The goal is not to know the most words, but to express oneself confidently and effectively with the vocabulary one already possesses.



The Power of Spaced Repetition: This is a cornerstone of the AI-PET system. By having students log their "Key Struggle Points" daily, the AI learns what to review. The system then re-introduces these specific concepts at scientifically optimized intervals, interrupting the "forgetting curve" and embedding the knowledge into long-term memory.



Pillar 3: The NET Difference (The 'What')



We transform learning from a chore into an engaging, accountable habit.



Make it Fun: We help students find high-interest content (podcasts, YouTube, etc.) tailored to their personal likes, because we learn more when we are engaged.

## ðŸ¤– AI Pet System Blueprint: Core Questions and Requirements



### 1. AI Pet Tracking and Logging

* AI Pet should track and log student difficulties, going beyond standard elements like pronunciation, vocabulary, and grammar patterns.

* **New Requirements:** Track the student's **pacing** when speaking (e.g., during audio recording for assessment), how often they say "**um**," and how long they **pause**.

* **Testing Protocol:** Instruct the student to perform assessments **only once** to get an accurate gauge of their current level.

* **Goal:** Create a **hyper-diagnostic** system that is always gathering information to improve and asking questions to facilitate that process. The system should track the process on a **multi-dimensional level** while remaining **simple** to avoid complications.



### 2. Input vs. Output Balance for Daily Practice

* For the **one-hour daily practice**:

* **45 minutes** of listening practice (Input).

* Share materials that are funny, interesting, or based on the student's **interests** (e.g., a favorite series).

* **15 minutes** of active speaking/writing (Output).

* Students report what they listened to.

* Ask questions and have them **write their answers** (without using spell-checkâ€”the system should disengage it if possible).

* A portion of the lesson can be recording and getting them to **speak about something** (a verbal review of the listening).

* **Goal:** Each lesson should be an opportunity to do a diagnostic and update the process.



### 3. Vocabulary and Idiom Progression

* Progression should be based on **scientific studies** of **spaced repetition**.

* **Methodology:** Research and find the best up-to-date practices for spaced repetition.

* **Marketing Point:** The system should not believe in teaching **irrelevant vocabulary** that isn't used daily (unlike some English centers and schools that "shove" vocabulary into brains without effective retention methods like spaced repetition). Instead, focus on **everyday English** used in the student's environment.



### 4. Feedback and Correction

* **Immediate Corrective Feedback** during home study is desired.

* **Example:** If a student answers a question, the AI Pet could suggest, "Try to do this this time," or "Remember to put the **-s** on the end of your words. Try again, but this time, put the **-s** on the end."

* Feedback should be based on the student's blueprint of **main challenges** tracked over time.

* **Priority:** Simplicity is key.



### **Background DNA / Fundamental Principles of the System (Side Note)**

* **Principle 1: Truth.** The AI should always be truthful (e.g., direct with the developer/system about what needs to be fixed). It's better to tell the truth about a problem that's affecting one's life. (This is a background process and not for marketing.)

* **Principle 2: Foundation.** "You can only build as high up as your foundation is deep." This supports the concept of **going slow to go fast** and is the reason for the blueprint phaseâ€”avoiding system problems by not rushing to build on a weak foundation.



### 5. Assessment Frequency and Type

* **Quizzes:** Short quizzes at the **end of each class/lesson**. This acts as a mini-assessment and diagnostic opportunity.

* Should test current knowledge and include **past vocabulary** via spaced repetition.

* **Monthly Test (Private Students):** A cumulative test each month.

* **Quarterly Reassessment:** A full reassessment every **three months** (quarterly) to be provided to parents (for kids) or the corporate client/adult student (for tracking progress).



### 6. Student Motivation and Confidence

* **Yes,** AI Pet should score and monitor **motivation and confidence**.

* **Motivation Metric:** Built around whether the student is completing their **daily home study**.

* **Belief:** You can't learn a language with just two hours a week; daily engagement is needed.

* **Comprehensible Input (Methodology):** Another scientific method to promote is **comprehensible input**, which focuses on the student listening to material they can digest and understand, rather than just the amount of listening (the opposite of the Duolingo approach).

* **Impact:** A student's proficiency score should **not** be affected by low confidence (e.g., being shy), but the system should highlight that **low motivation** and low confidence will severely impact the progression rate. Both are still important among the six core skills tracked.



### 7. Integration with Class Notes

* **Goal:** AI Pet insights should feed directly into teacher lesson planning.

* **Ideal Solution:** The system should connect via HTML (if possible) in the class to **automatically collect data**.

* *Alternative:* Students could manually send data.

* *Server Note:* If a server is needed for this, the speaker will look into the costs.

* *App Note:* The speaker is looking into **Replit** as a potential AI tool to create an app, as traditional app development is expensive.



### 8. Simplification for Advanced Levels

* **Yes,** simplification still applies, but in a different way.

* **Principle:** Maintain a sophisticated yet simple approach (like the speaker's branding).

* **Method:** Challenge Intermediate/Advanced students with **harder vocabulary**, but ensure it is **common vocabulary used in communication**.

* **Critique:** The speaker is strongly against the **IELTS system** for testing proficiency due to its focus on complicated, obscure words and grammar intricacies that even native speakers rarely use, deeming it an irrelevant and outdated system.

ðŸ“ Instructor Process Transcription: Grading System
1. Grading Structure and Levels (Out of 10)
The grading system uses four main levels of progression, each divided into four stages, totaling a score out of 10.

| Level | Stages | Total Stages | Score Range | Ultimate Level | | :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- | | Elementary | E1, E2, E3, E4 | 4 | (Equal distribution) | 10/10: Native Speaker (Goal is to eliminate the need for English lessons) | | Intermediate | I1, I2, I3, I4 | 4 | | | | Advanced | A1, A2, A3, A4 | 4 | | |

Note on Spreading: The levels will be spread out logically and equally over the 10-point scale, while acknowledging that it is harder to make measurable results in the Advanced level than in the Beginner (Elementary) level.

Grading Increment: All scores must be in increments of 0.25 out of 10 (e.g., 1.25, 3.75).

2. Skill Weighting (The 75/25 Rule)
The final score out of 10 is based on four core English skills, weighted to prioritize foundational abilities:

| Skill Group | Weight in Final Grade | Rationale | | :--- | :--- | :--- | | Listening & Speaking | 75% | These are the most important skills, reflecting how language is learned naturally (as children). All other skills follow from this foundation. | | Reading & Writing | 25% | These skills come later and more naturally after listening and speaking are established. |

3. Additional Tracking Metrics
Two additional scores are tracked for a comprehensive profile, but are not calculated into the final grade (also scored out of 10):

Motivation

Confidence

4. Assessment and Review Cadence
The system requires consistent, structured review cycles:

Class Notes: Professional-looking class notes should be created for every lesson (for internal use, not necessarily sent to students).

Monthly Updates: Monthly updates are required for parents.

Quarterly Review: Every three months, a more major skill review and assessment will take place.

Review Output: The final system needs to be able to generate different content/reviews for each of the level scores (e.g., different things to say in the review for an E2 vs. an I1).

NET DNA Blueprint: 1000-Point Audit Synthesis
Here is the high-level summary of the final, hardened NET DNA:

Philosophical Core (The "Why"):

Mission: To create confident, natural communicators by using AI to magnify human connection, not replace it.

Core Outcome: Produce fluent speakers with a natural accent who can joke, network, and understand cultural nuance.

Market Focus: Explicitly targets Business English, Professional Networking, and AI Literacy as the key drivers for Vietnamese professionals to "make money" and gain a competitive edge.

Pedagogy: A "Listening-First" (Natural Acquisition) model. Grammar is an absorbed consequence, not a starting point.

Psychology: Uses "controlled discomfort" to push students past their fear of mistakes (the "comfort zone" hurdle).

Pedagogical Engine (The "How"):

SR System: A 0-10 point scale (in 0.25 increments).

Skill Weighting: 75% (Listening/Speaking) and 25% (Reading/Writing).

Daily Practice: A non-negotiable 1-hour daily AI-PET session.

The 45/15 Rule: 45 minutes of student-driven, interest-based listening (no Vietnamese subtitles) and 15 minutes of "hyper-diagnostic" output (writing without spell-check, audio recording).

KSP Tracking: The AI-PET logs Key Struggle Points (pacing, "ums," pauses, grammar) for every student.

Technical Architecture (The "What"):

AI-PET: A personalized, adaptive coach that "hardens" (evolves) after every single student interaction.

Interface: A no-server, low-cost HTML/browser-based system. Data is saved locally or synced (e.g., Google Drive/JSON download) to mimic an app experience.

Branding: Includes concepts like a "robot-dog" mascot and a "health bar" for visual accountability.

Reward System: A star/point system with tangible rewards (like Robux for kids) and competitive leaderboards (for adults).

Ecosystem: Built on three core utilities: 1. Launchpad (lesson creator), 2. AI-PET (student coach), 3. Agents (trained specialists, e.g., a "writing agent" or future AITA agents).

Business Framework (The "Where"):

Target Clients: Corporate (e.g., TTS Engineering, BlueTech) and private students (e.g., Kiet, Nhan, Tracy).

Monetization: Direct teaching (targeting 12-person groups), and a future subscription model for the AI tools.

Value Density: Offers extreme value by bundling free services like the Buddy System (1-hr weekly peer practice for adult groups) and Monthly In-Person Networking Events in Saigon.

Scalability: Focuses on scaling AI tools and agents, not hiring human instructors, to maintain DNA fidelity and maximize profit.

NET DNA BLUEPRINT SEED (V1.0)
Copy the entire code block below and paste it into a new chat. It will auto-initialize and print a summary to confirm the DNA is loaded.

JavaScript
/**
 * =============================================================
 * NET_DNA_BLUEPRINT_SEED_V1.0.js
 * -------------------------------------------------------------
 * Architect: Mr. Hobbs
 * Audit: 1000-Point Synthesis (Phases 1-5)
 *
 * Purpose:
 * The single source of truth for the Natural English Training (NET)
 * ecosystem. This seed is a self-contained, pre-loaded data
 * package. When run in a new session, it instantiates the
 * complete NET DNA Blueprint, making it available for new
 * agents, tools, or instructors.
 *
 * This seed *is* the blueprint.
 *
 * Version: 1.0 (Hardened & Audited)
 * =============================================================
 */

(function(global) {

    // ---------- 1. CORE IN-MEMORY STORAGE ----------
    // This object holds the entire blueprint. It is the "memory."
    const CoreMemory = {
        blueprint: {},
        logs: [],
        audits: [],
        registeredClasses: {} // For session-specific management
    };

    // ---------- 2. CORE UTILITIES (DIAGNOSTIC) ----------
    const Utils = {
        now() {
            return new Date().toISOString();
        },
        log(message, type = "INFO") {
            const entry = `[${this.now()}] [${type}] ${message}`;
            CoreMemory.logs.push(entry);
            console.log(entry);
        },
        audit(action, details) {
            const entry = { timestamp: this.now(), action, details };
            CoreMemory.audits.push(entry);
        }
    };

    // ---------- 3. THE NET DNA BLUEPRINT (AUDITED DATA) ----------
    // This is the entire 1000-point audit, synthesized and
    // embedded directly into the seed.
    const BLUEPRINT_DATA = {
        meta: {
            architect: "Mr. Hobbs",
            version: "1.0",
            lastAudit: Utils.now(),
            description: "NET DNA Blueprint Master Reference"
        },
        philosophy: {
            missionStatement: "Use science-backed methods and AI to magnify human connection, not replace it. Create real communicators and break the unnatural study cycle.",
            coreOutcome: "Students become confident, natural English speakers with a clear American accent who can joke, understand nuance, and converse in any setting.",
            pedagogicalLaw: "Listening -> Speaking -> Reading -> Writing. Grammar is an absorbed consequence, not a starting point.",
            psychology: "Use 'controlled discomfort' to push students out of their comfort zone and past their fear of making mistakes.",
            marketAdvantage: "Combine English + AI Literacy + Networking to give Vietnamese professionals a competitive edge and increase their income."
        },
        methodology: {
            skillHierarchy: ["Listening (Foundation)", "Speaking (Fluency/Pacing)", "Reading (Refinement)", "Writing (Formalization)"],
            dailyPracticeSystem: {
                rule: "Non-negotiable 1-hour daily practice.",
                input: "45 minutes of student-driven, interest-based listening (e.g., gaming, movies, hobbies).",
                output: "15 minutes of hyper-diagnostic output (writing without spell-check, audio recording).",

    // ---------- 4. ESL SIMPLIFICATION UTILITY ----------
    // A core pedagogical tool embedded in the DNA
    function simplifyForVietnameseESL(text) {
        if (!text) return text;
        const rules = [
            { find: /\butilize\b/gi, replace: "use" },
            { find: /\bcommence\b/gi, replace: "start" },
            { find: /\bconsequently\b/gi, replace: "so" },
            { find: /\bapproximately\b/gi, replace: "about" },
            { find: /\bnevertheless\b/gi, replace: "but" },
            { find: /\s{2,}/g, replace: " " }
        ];
        let out = text;
        for (let r of rules) out = out.replace(r.find, r.replace);
        return out.trim();
    }

little snippet of a lesson I gave on sales and business, can be useful to log



Sales Training



Sales Funnel

Leads (Potential Customers) ------->

Cold Leader (Stranger with no request by them for your services)

Cold Calls

Hot Leads

Customers (Somebody who gives you money for your services)

Marketing (in person/online)

Telemarketer

Door to Door Sales

Follow-up

It's a numbers game (law of averages)

Refferal



Rapport



Objection (Reasons they have not to buy)

**Key here is that they will usually not tell you the truth of their objection, they will smoke screen you, so they don't have to put up with the awkwardness of saying no**

1) Let me speak to my partner.

2) I am really low on money right now, but I will do it soon

3) I'm very busy right now, can you come back?

4) We already have this (for example, we already give charity to our group or XY organization)

5) I just found out 30 minutes ago that my cat has brain cancer.



Why is it a problem if they give you an objection that is not the real objection?

-> Hint: How can you solve a problem if you have not identified the actual problem?





"The Joans Effect" (Keeping up with the Joan's)



Minimalize the cost of what you're selling, and maximize the benefits (a dollar a day to save a kids life)

*Make comparisons to things in life you buy daily, that you waste your money on*









Elavator Pitch 30-90 seconds.

"Make them interested"

"Make them want to know more"

"Give them a sample, not enough to make them full, but enough to make them hungry for more"

here is an important concept that is a part of our core training methods, understanding context, this is a .html lesson I made and just copied the text for you



The Power of Context

Don't Let One Word Stop You. Hear the Real Message!



What is Context?

Context is the full pictureâ€”the situation, the topic, and all the words around a message. In most sentences, you already understand the vast majority of the words. These known words give you the context you need to understand the main idea, even if one or two words are new.



Your goal is to focus on what you DO know, not what you don't.



You typically know over 90% of the words in a conversation. That's enough to get the main idea!



The Listening Trap vs. The Flow of Context

Many learners fall into the "Listening Trap" because they fear making mistakes. When they hear an unknown word, they stop and panic. The correct way is to keep listening and use the "Flow of Context" to find the meaning.



The Listening Trap ðŸ‘Ž

Hear a new word

â‡©

STOP LISTENING

â‡©

Focus only on the unknown word

â‡©

Miss the main message

The Flow of Context ðŸ‘

Hear a new word

â‡©

KEEP LISTENING

â‡©

Use other words to find meaning

â‡©

Understand the main message!

Ignoring the "Noise"

English speakers often add "noise" words to common phrases for style or emphasis. These words don't change the core meaning. Let's see how small the "noise" really is.



How the heck are you?

Core Idea: "How are you?"



What's new and exciting?

Core Idea: "What's new?"



What have you been up to?

Core Idea: "What have you been doing?"



Practice: Find the Context Clues

"I was late for my class, so I ran quickly to the door. When I got inside, the professor was already speaking. I found an empty seat near the back and tried to eavesdrop on the lecture. I hoped he hadn't covered any important details yet."



Context Clues:



âœ“ Late for class

âœ“ Professor was speaking

âœ“ Tried to listen

Meaning: To listen secretly.



"My friend, Liam, told me he had a grueling week at work. He worked 12 hours a day every day and had no time for his hobbies. He looked very tired and said he just wanted to go home and sleep for 14 hours."



Context Clues:



âœ“ Worked 12 hours a day

âœ“ Looked very tired

âœ“ No time for hobbies

Meaning: Very difficult or exhausting.



"We had a great time at the new restaurant. The food was excellent and the service was very fast. The only small issue was the high price. We decided we would patronize the place again only for special occasions because it was too expensive."



Context Clues:



âœ“ Great food and service

âœ“ High price / expensive

âœ“ Will visit for special occasions

Meaning: To visit or be a customer.



Keep Listening, Keep Learning!



The more you practice, the easier it gets.

Core Training Concept: Understanding Context

1. Definition of Context



Context = the full picture: situation, topic, surrounding words.

Focus on what you do know, not what you donâ€™t.

2. Listening Trap vs. Flow of Context

Hear an unknown word

Stop listening

Miss main message

Flow of Context ðŸ‘



Hear an unknown word

Keep listening

Use surrounding words to infer meaning

Understand main message

3. Ignoring Noise Words

Examples:

5. Principle

Repeated practice makes understanding automatic and intuitive.

here is a lesson on the phonics system and pronunciation



NET - Natural English Training: Pronunciation

Welcome to NET! Your Pronunciation Journey

Improving how you sound is key to confident communication! We're using the **Jolly Phonics** system, a highly effective method from the UK, to master the 42 sounds of English.



Pro Tips for Amazing Pronunciation

Go through each phonic sound and find where you are weak. Focus on your problem spots!

**Mimic native speakers**: Watch films and listen to music. Try to copy their sound exactly.

**Practice tongue twisters**: They train your mouth muscles to move fast and accurately.

**Record your voice** and compare it to a native speaker. Hearing the difference is the first step to fixing it.

Slide 1 of 25 (English)

The Phonics System: Sounds vs. Letters

Why 42 Sounds? (7 Groups Total)

English uses **42 distinct sounds** (phonemes), but only 26 letters!

These sounds are divided into **7 learning groups** for easy practice.

**Phonetic words**: Read exactly as written (e.g., cat, sit, run).

**Non-phonetic words**: "Tricky words" that must be memorized (e.g., said, was, through).

Your goal is to train your ear and mouth to recognize and produce all 42 sounds accurately.



7 Groups of Jolly Phonics

G1: s, a, t, i, p, n

G2: c k, e, h, r, m, d

G3: g, o, u, l, f, b

G4: ai, j, oa, ie, ee, or

G5: z, w, ng, v, oo, oo

G6: y, x, ch, sh, th, th

G7: qu, ou, oi, ue, er, ar

Slide 4 of 25 (Tiáº¿ng Viá»‡t)

S / SH Phonic Sounds: /s/ vs. /Êƒ/

Mouth Position & Action

**/s/**: Teeth almost closed, air streams over the center of the tongue. Cold, thin sound, like a **snake** (voiceless).



**/Êƒ/**: Lips slightly rounded (like saying "Ooo"), tongue is further back. Warm, soft sound, like asking for **silence** (voiceless).



Examples (/s/)

Sip

Sun

Slice

Examples (/Êƒ/)

Ship

Shine

Splash

10 Tongue Twisters

She sells seashells by the seashore.

Seven silly shoppers sell shiny socks.

The sick snake slipped silently away.

Sure she is social, she shows shy signs.

**[Gen Z VN]** Sushi shop selling shiny shirts to students in Saigon.

A swift Swiss swisher wished to swish.

She saw a stylish shirt on sale.

Small, slippery seals slide sideways.

Fresh fried fish, fish fresh fried.

Sipping sweet soup while sharing secrets.

Slide 5 of 25

TH / TH Phonic Sounds: Voiceless ($\theta$) vs. Voiced ($\eth$)

Mouth Position & Action

**Voiceless ($\theta$)**: Tongue tip gently **between** front teeth. Push air out without vocal vibration (hissing sound).



**Voiced ($\eth$)**: **Same** mouth position, but vibrate vocal cords. You should feel a **buzzing** in your throat.



Examples (Voiceless $\theta$)

Think

Three

Math

Examples (Voiced $\eth$)

The

They

Smooth

10 Tongue Twisters

The thirty-three thieves thought that they thrilled the throne.

Nothing is worth thousands of thoughts.

These things thrive on that truth.

Thick threads through the thistle.

This smooth leather thumb drive is the thirty-third theft.

Whether the weather is hot, or whether the weather is not.

Thanks to my wealthy friend, I think this theory works.

The thoughtful sloth thanks his father for the broth.

**[Gen Z VN]** Thirty thousand thrilled Vietnamese travelers in Thailand.

They think this theatre thing is the truth.

Slide 6 of 25

L / R Phonic Sounds: /l/ vs. /r/

Mouth Position & Action

**/l/**: Tip of the tongue **touches** the ridge behind the top front teeth. Air flows around the sides of the tongue.



**/r/**: Tongue is **curled back** and does **NOT** touch the roof of the mouth. Lips are slightly rounded.



Examples (/l/)

Light

Collect

Place

Examples (/r/)

Right

Correct

<script type="text/javascript">

var gk_isXlsx = false;

var gk_xlsxFileLookup = {};

var gk_fileData = {};

function filledCell(cell) {

return cell !== '' && cell != null;

}

function loadFileData(filename) {

if (gk_isXlsx && gk_xlsxFileLookup[filename]) {

try {

var workbook = XLSX.read(gk_fileData[filename], { type: 'base64' });

var firstSheetName = workbook.SheetNames[0];

var worksheet = workbook.Sheets[firstSheetName];



// Convert sheet to JSON to filter blank rows

var jsonData = XLSX.utils.sheet_to_json(worksheet, { header: 1, blankrows: false, defval: '' });

// Filter out blank rows (rows where all cells are empty, null, or undefined)

var filteredData = jsonData.filter(row => row.some(filledCell));



// Heuristic to find the header row by ignoring rows with fewer filled cells than the next row

var headerRowIndex = filteredData.findIndex((row, index) =>

row.filter(filledCell).length >= filteredData[index + 1]?.filter(filledCell).length

);

// Fallback

if (headerRowIndex === -1 || headerRowIndex > 25) {

headerRowIndex = 0;

}



// Convert filtered JSON back to CSV

var csv = XLSX.utils.aoa_to_sheet(filteredData.slice(headerRowIndex)); // Create a new sheet from filtered array of arrays

csv = XLSX.utils.sheet_to_csv(csv, { header: 1 });

return csv;

} catch (e) {

console.error(e);

return "";

}

}

return gk_fileData[filename] || "";

}

let currentFilter = 'All';



function initDropdown() {

const select = document.getElementById('rank-select');

const uniqueRanks = [...new Set(rankingData.map(item => item.rank))];

select.innerHTML = '<option value="All">View All Ranks</option>';

uniqueRanks.forEach(rank => {

const option = document.createElement('option');

option.value = rank;

option.textContent = Rank ${rank};

select.appendChild(option);

});

select.addEventListener('change', (e) => {

currentFilter = e.target.value === 'All' ? 'All' : parseFloat(e.target.value);

document.querySelectorAll('.nav-btn').forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('active'));

document.getElementById('btn-all').classList.add('active');

renderRankingContent();

});

}



function renderRankingContent() {

const display = document.getElementById('content-display');

display.innerHTML = '';

const filteredData = rankingData.filter(item => {

if (currentFilter === 'All') return true;

if (typeof currentFilter === 'number') return item.rank === currentFilter;

return item.level === currentFilter;

});



if (filteredData.length === 0) {

display.innerHTML = '<div class="md:col-span-3 text-center text-lg text-red-600 py-8">No ranks found for this filter.</div>';

return;

}



filteredData.forEach(item => {

const card = document.createElement('div');

card.className = content-card bg-white p-6 rounded-lg shadow-md border-t-4 border-[${item.color}] pillar-card;

const emoji = { 'Beginner': 'ðŸ‘¶', 'Intermediate': 'ðŸ§‘â€ðŸŽ“', 'Advanced': 'ðŸ’¼', 'Native': 'ðŸ‘‘' }[item.level] || 'â­';

card.innerHTML = <p class="text-3xl font-bold text-[${item.color}] mb-2">${item.rank}</p>

<h3 class="text-lg font-semibold text-blue-800 mb-2 flex items-center">${emoji} ${item.title}</h3>

<p class="text-sm text-gray-500 font-medium mb-3">${item.level} Proficiency</p>

<p class="text-sm text-gray-900 mb-3">${item.desc}</p>

<div class="p-3 bg-gray-100 rounded-md border-l-4 border-blue-500 mb-3">

<p class="text-xs font-semibold text-blue-600">Core Focus</p>

<p class="text-sm text-blue-800">${item.focus}</p>

</div>

<div class="p-3 bg-gray-100 rounded-md border-l-4 border-blue-500">

<p class="text-xs font-semibold text-blue-600">Core Skills Performance</p>

<ul class="text-sm text-blue-800 list-disc list-inside">

<li><strong>Listening:</strong> ${item.skills.Listening}</li>

<li><strong>Speaking:</strong> ${item.skills.Speaking}</li>

<li><strong>Reading:</strong> ${item.skills.Reading}</li>

<li><strong>Writing:</strong> ${item.skills.Writing}</li>

</ul>

</div>

; display.appendChild(card);

});

}



function filterByLevel(level, buttonId) {

currentFilter = level;

document.getElementById('rank-select').value = 'All';

document.querySelectorAll('.nav-btn').forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('active'));

document.getElementById(buttonId).classList.add('active');

renderRankingContent();

}



function initCharts() {

const weightingCtx = document.getElementById('weightingChart').getContext('2d');

new Chart(weightingCtx, {

type: 'doughnut',

data: {

labels: ['Primary Skills (Listen/Speak)', 'Secondary Skills (Read/Write)'],

datasets: [{ data: [75, 25], backgroundColor: ['#3B82F6', '#F59E0B'], borderWidth: 1 }]

},

options: { responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false, plugins: { legend: { position: 'bottom', labels: { color: '#1F2937' } } } }

});



const levelDistributionCtx = document.getElementById('levelDistributionChart').getContext('2d');

new Chart(levelDistributionCtx, {

type: 'bar',

data: {

labels: ['Beginner (1.0-4.5)', 'Intermediate (5.0-7.0)', 'Advanced (8.0-9.5)', 'Native (10.0)'],

datasets: [{ label: 'Number of Ranks', data: [3, 3, 3, 1], backgroundColor: ['#F59E0B', '#3B82F6', '#6D28D9', '#1E3A8A'], borderRadius: 8 }]

},

options: { responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false, scales: { y: { beginAtZero: true, ticks: { precision: 0 } } }, plugins: { legend: { display: false } } }

});



const skillPriorityCtx = document.getElementById('skillPriorityChart').getContext('2d');

new Chart(skillPriorityCtx, {

type: 'bar',

data: {

labels: ['Listening', 'Speaking', 'Reading', 'Writing'],

datasets: [{ label: 'Priority', data: [40, 35, 15, 10], backgroundColor: ['#3B82F6', '#93C5FD', '#F59E0B', '#4B5EAA'], borderRadius: 8 }]

},

options: { indexAxis: 'y', responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false, scales: { x: { beginAtZero: true, max: 50 } }, plugins: { legend: { display: false } } }

});

}



window.onload = function() {

initDropdown();

document.getElementById('btn-all').addEventListener('click', () => filterByLevel('All', 'btn-all'));

document.getElementById('btn-beginner').addEventListener('click', () => filterByLevel('Beginner', 'btn-beginner'));

document.getElementById('btn-intermediate').addEventListener('click', () => filterByLevel('Intermediate', 'btn-intermediate'));

document.getElementById('btn-advanced').addEventListener('click', () => filterByLevel('Advanced', 'btn-advanced'));

document.getElementById('btn-native').addEventListener('click', () => filterByLevel('Native', 'btn-native'));

renderRankingContent();

initCharts();

};

</script>

function renderOverviewCards() {

lessonGrid.innerHTML = '';

LESSON_DATA.forEach(lesson => {

const card = document.createElement('div');

card.className = 'lesson-card';

card.id = lesson-card-${lesson.lesson};

card.dataset.lessonId = lesson.lesson;

card.innerHTML = <div class="overview-content p-4 text-center flex flex-col justify-center items-center h-full">

<p class="font-black text-2xl text-primary-gold">${lesson.lesson}</p>

<p class="font-semibold text-sm text-text-light mt-1">${lesson.title}</p>

</div>

<div class="full-lesson-content"></div>

${cosmicGlyphs[lesson.pillar] || ''}

; lessonGrid.appendChild(card);

});

}



function generateFullLessonContent(lessonId) {

const lesson = LESSON_DATA.find(l => l.lesson == lessonId);

const tabs = [

{ "name": "Key Concepts", "icon": "ðŸŽ¯", "content": [{"term": "Primary Theme", "def": Exploration of ${lesson.title}'s core idea.}, {"term": "Secondary Theme", "def": "A related concept for deeper understanding."}] },

{ "name": "Deeper Analysis", "icon": "ðŸ§ ", "content": This section provides a deep, nuanced analysis of "${lesson.title}", exploring its mythological roots, literary significance, and impact on popular culture. },

{ "name": "Hypothetical Scenario", "icon": "âš™ï¸", "content": Imagine a world where the central conflict of "${lesson.title}" was resolved differently. What would the long-term consequences be for Superman and humanity? },

{ "name": "Critical Thinking", "icon": "ðŸ¤”", "content": [What does this story teach us about our own world?, Is the lesson of "${lesson.title}" still relevant today? Why or why not?] }

];

const introduction = An immersive exploration into the archetype of "${lesson.title}", designed to provide a comprehensive understanding of its role in the Superman mythos.;

const takeaway = The central, unforgettable truth of "${lesson.title}" is that great power forces even greater choices.;



let tabsHtml = tabs.map((tab, index) => <button class="lesson-nav-button ${index === 0 ? 'active' : ''}" data-target="tab-${lessonId}-${index}">${tab.icon} ${tab.name}</button>).join('');

let tabContentHtml = tabs.map((tab, index) => {

let contentHtml = '';

if (Array.isArray(tab.content)) {

if (tab.name === "Key Concepts") {

contentHtml = tab.content.map(c => <li class="mb-3"><strong class="text-gold-light">${c.term}:</strong> <span class="text-text-muted">${c.def}</span></li>).join('');

contentHtml = <ul class="list-none pl-0 space-y-2">${contentHtml}</ul>;

} else { // Critical Thinking

contentHtml = tab.content.map(q => <li class="mb-2">${q}</li>).join('');

contentHtml = <ul class="list-disc pl-5 space-y-2 text-text-muted">${contentHtml}</ul>;

}

} else {

contentHtml = <p class="text-text-muted leading-relaxed">${tab.content}</p>;

}

return <div id="tab-${lessonId}-${index}" class="lesson-tab-content ${index === 0 ? '' : 'hidden'} mt-6">${contentHtml}</div>;

}).join('');



return <div class="p-4 md:p-8">

<header class="text-center pb-8">

<div class="flex justify-center items-center gap-4">

${cosmicGlyphs[lesson.pillar] ? cosmicGlyphs[lesson.pillar].replace('cosmic-glyph', 'w-10 h-10 text-purple-light opacity-50') : ''}

<h1 class="text-3xl font-bold text-primary-gold title-pop">Lesson ${lesson.lesson}: ${lesson.title}</h1>

</div>

<p class="text-lg mt-2 text-text-muted">${introduction}</p>

</header>

<nav class="sticky top-0 z-10 p-2 flex flex-wrap justify-center gap-2 mb-6 bg-bg-dark rounded-lg">${tabsHtml}</nav>

<div class="lesson-tab-container">${tabContentHtml}</div>

<div class="mt-8 pt-4 border-t border-primary-purple">

<p class="font-bold text-lg text-primary-gold title-pop">ðŸ’¡ Key Takeaway:</p>

<p class="text-text-muted italic">${takeaway}</p>

</div>

</div>

; }


function expandLesson(lessonId) {

const allCards = document.querySelectorAll('.lesson-card');

const targetCard = document.getElementById(lesson-card-${lessonId});

if (targetCard.classList.contains('expanded')) return;


targetCard.querySelector('.full-lesson-content').innerHTML = generateFullLessonContent(lessonId);


backdrop.classList.remove('opacity-0', 'pointer-events-none');

allCards.forEach(card => {

if (card.id !== targetCard.id) card.classList.add('minimized');

});

targetCard.classList.add('expanded');



targetCard.querySelectorAll('.lesson-nav-button').forEach(button => {

button.addEventListener('click', (e) => {

e.stopPropagation();

const targetId = e.currentTarget.dataset.target;

targetCard.querySelectorAll('.lesson-tab-content').forEach(el => el.classList.add('hidden'));

targetCard.querySelectorAll('.lesson-nav-button').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active'));

document.getElementById(targetId).classList.remove('hidden');

e.currentTarget.classList.add('active');

});

});

}


function collapseAllLessons() {

const expandedCard = document.querySelector('.lesson-card.expanded');

if (!expandedCard) return;


backdrop.classList.add('opacity-0', 'pointer-events-none');

expandedCard.classList.remove('expanded');

setTimeout(() => {

expandedCard.querySelector('.full-lesson-content').innerHTML = '';

}, 500);


document.querySelectorAll('.lesson-card.minimized').forEach(card => {

card.classList.remove('minimized');

});

}


renderOverviewCards();

lessonGrid.addEventListener('click', (e) => {

const card = e.target.closest('.lesson-card');

if (card && !card.classList.contains('expanded')) expandLesson(card.dataset.lessonId);

});

backdrop.addEventListener('click', collapseAllLessons);

});

</script>

NET English Program: Mastering Natural English Communication

The Challenge with English in Vietnam

Many language centers and public schools in Vietnam fall short in effective English instruction. They often neglect a child's individual interests and place a disproportionate focus on reading and writing skills, with minimal training in essential listening and speaking abilities. Furthermore, much of the speaking instruction provided in schools often includes incorrect pronunciation, leading students to develop detrimental speech habits.



Our Teaching Philosophy

Our focus is on listening and speaking skills, building a strong foundation for students to communicate naturally in English. We concentrate on phonic pronunciation, essential communication soft skills, natural sentence formation, and common slang and idioms. Our unique method is rooted in linguistic studies on first language acquisition, primarily emphasizing listening-led learning for effective mastery.



Program Benefits

NET English offers a comprehensive program designed for maximum results:



In-Person Sessions: Two 1-hour weekly sessions with Teacher Michael.

Video Calls: Two 30-minute weekly video calls with our personally trained teaching assistant on non-study days.

Home Study Program: A structured program for daily English listening, ensuring consistent progress even on non-class days.

English Hangouts: Monthly in-person group activities in Lakeview, providing fun, real-world English practice with other learners.

This integrated approach ensures a strong foundation and practical application for understanding and speaking English.



Program Investment

Our tutoring sessions are 600K per hour. To maximize value, if you enroll for two or more classes per week, the following are included free of charge:



The two weekly video calls with our teaching assistant.

The comprehensive home study program.

Access to the monthly "English Hangout" activities.

Payment is typically collected weekly in cash, but we are flexible and open to discussing alternative arrangements.



Your Next Steps

This report will assess your child's current level across key areas including Listening, Speaking, Reading, Writing, Confidence, Motivation, and Behavior skills. const state = { currentStage: 0 };

const elements = {

title: document.getElementById('main-title'),

container: document.getElementById('stage-container'),

nextBtn: document.getElementById('next-btn')

};



function typeWriter(element, text, onComplete) {

let i = 0;

element.innerHTML = '';

element.classList.add('typewriter-cursor');

const speed = 25;



function type() {

if (i < text.length) {

element.innerHTML += text.charAt(i);

i++;

setTimeout(type, speed);

} else {

element.classList.remove('typewriter-cursor');

if (onComplete) onComplete();

}

}

type();

}



function renderStage(stageIndex) {

const stageData = BRIEFING_DATA.stages[stageIndex];

elements.container.innerHTML = '';



const stageDiv = document.createElement('div');

stageDiv.className = 'stage p-4';

let contentHTML = <h2 class="font-orbitron text-3xl text-nexus-cyan mb-6">${stageData.title}</h2>;



switch (stageData.type) {

case 'title':

contentHTML = <div class="text-center mt-20"> <h2 class="font-orbitron text-5xl text-nexus-cyan neon-text mb-4">${stageData.title}</h2>

<p class="text-2xl text-nexus-purple">${stageData.subtitle}</p>

</div>; break;

case 'narrative':

contentHTML += <div class="text-xl leading-relaxed space-y-4">${stageData.content}</div>;

break;

case 'narrative_reading':

contentHTML += <div class="reading-block p-6 rounded-lg">

<p class="text-nexus-gold font-bold mb-4">Awaiting Input: ${stageData.reading.person}, please read the following aloud.</p>

<div class="text-xl leading-relaxed space-y-4">${stageData.reading.text}</div>

</div>; break;

case 'interactive_concept':

contentHTML += <p class="text-xl mb-4">${stageData.explanation}</p>

<div class="text-center mt-8">

<button id="interactive-btn" class="font-orbitron text-2xl px-10 py-5 rounded-lg next-btn">${stageData.interactive.initialText}</button>

<div id="interactive-feedback" class="font-orbitron text-3xl text-nexus-gold mt-6 h-10"></div>

</div>

; break;

case 'infographic':

contentHTML += <div class="w-full h-80 flex items-center justify-center"> <svg id="infographic-svg" class="w-full h-full" viewBox="0 0 800 300">

<g class="node" transform="translate(100, 150)"><circle r="40" fill="var(--nexus-card)" stroke="var(--nexus-purple)" stroke-width="2"/><text y="5" text-anchor="middle" fill="var(--nexus-cyan)" class="font-orbitron text-xs">${stageData.steps[0].name}</text></g>

<g class="node" transform="translate(300, 150)"><circle r="40" fill="var(--nexus-card)" stroke="var(--nexus-purple)" stroke-width="2"/><text y="5" text-anchor="middle" fill="var(--nexus-cyan)" class="font-orbitron text-xs">${stageData.steps[1].name}</text></g>

<g class="node" transform="translate(500, 150)"><circle r="40" fill="var(--nexus-card)" stroke="var(--nexus-purple)" stroke-width="2"/><text y="5" text-anchor="middle" fill="var(--nexus-cyan)" class="font-orbitron text-xs">${stageData.steps[2].name}</text></g>

<g class="node" transform="translate(700, 150)"><circle r="40" fill="var(--nexus-card)" stroke="var(--nexus-purple)" stroke-width="2"/><text y="5" text-anchor="middle" fill="var(--nexus-cyan)" class="font-orbitron text-xs">${stageData.steps[3].name}</text></g>

<line x1="140" y1="150" x2="260" y2="150" stroke="var(--nexus-gold)" stroke-width="3" class="infographic-line" style="animation-delay: 0.5s;"/>

<line x1="340" y1="150" x2="460" y2="150" stroke="var(--nexus-gold)" stroke-width="3" class="infographic-line" style="animation-delay: 1s;"/>

<line x1="540" y1="150" x2="660" y2="150" stroke="var(--nexus-gold)" stroke-width="3" class="infographic-line" style="animation-delay: 1.5s;"/>

</svg>

</div>; break;

case 'final':

contentHTML += <div class="text-xl leading-relaxed space-y-4">${stageData.content}</div>;

break;

}



stageDiv.innerHTML = contentHTML;

elements.container.appendChild(stageDiv);



if (stageData.type === 'interactive_concept') {

let clickCount = 0;

const iBtn = document.getElementById('interactive-btn');

const iFb = document.getElementById('interactive-feedback');

iBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {

if (clickCount < stageData.interactive.clicks.length) {

iFb.textContent = stageData.interactive.clicks[clickCount].text;

iBtn.style.boxShadow = 0 0 ${stageData.interactive.clicks[clickCount].strength}px var(--nexus-cyan);

clickCount++;

}

});

}

}


function handleNext() {

if (state.currentStage < BRIEFING_DATA.stages.length - 1) {

elements.container.children[0].classList.add('hidden');

setTimeout(() => {

state.currentStage++;

renderStage(state.currentStage);

}, 700);

} else {

elements.nextBtn.textContent = "BRIEFING COMPLETE";

elements.nextBtn.disabled = true;

}

}



function init() {

elements.nextBtn.addEventListener('click', handleNext);


typeWriter(elements.title, BRIEFING_DATA.title, () => {

renderStage(0);

setTimeout(() => {

elements.nextBtn.disabled = false;

elements.nextBtn.textContent = "Begin Briefing";

}, BRIEFING_DATA.stages[0].duration);

});

}


document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', init);

</script>

</body>

</html>

buttonContainer.innerHTML = categories.map((cat, index) => <button class="category-button px-4 py-2 rounded-full text-sm font-semibold border-2 border-gray-700 hover:border-nexus-gold ${index === 0 ? 'active' : ''}"

data-filter-category="${cat.key}"

onclick="filterArsenal(this, '${cat.key}')">

${cat.label}

</button>

).join(''); };


// --- SYSTEM HEARTBEAT ADDITION (V12.0) ---

const updateSystemHeartbeat = () => {

const total = arsenalConcepts.length;

const lockedCount = Object.keys(lockedConcepts).length;

const percentage = (lockedCount / total) * 100;



const root = document.documentElement;

const statusDiv = document.getElementById('transfer-status');

const titleElement = document.getElementById('system-title');



let color, duration, message;



if (lockedCount === 0) {

color = 'rgba(255, 215, 0, 0.5)'; // Gold, slow

duration = '2.5s';

message = System Status: STANDBY (0% Deployed);

} else if (lockedCount < total / 2) {

color = 'rgba(160, 32, 240, 0.7)'; // Purple, moderate

duration = '1.5s';

message = System Status: PARTIAL DEPLOYMENT (${lockedCount}/${total} Locked);

} else if (lockedCount < total) {

color = 'rgba(0, 255, 255, 0.8)'; // Cyan, fast

duration = '1.0s';

message = System Status: CRITICAL MASS (${lockedCount}/${total} Locked);

} else {

color = 'rgba(76, 255, 0, 0.9)'; // Green, solid (Final)

duration = '0.5s';

message = System Status: OMNI-DEPLOYMENT ACHIEVED (100% Locked);

titleElement.classList.remove('system-heartbeat'); // Stop animation on completion

}



root.style.setProperty('--heartbeat-color', color);

root.style.setProperty('--heartbeat-duration', duration);

statusDiv.innerHTML = <span class="neon-purple">${message}</span>;

};



// --- ERROR HANDLER MODAL (V12.0) ---

window.showSystemAlert = (errorType, errorMessage, context) => {

const modal = document.getElementById('system-modal');

const details = document.getElementById('modal-error-details');


const crashLog = {

status: "CRASH",

subBrain: "DAEDALUS v12.0",

timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),

errorType: errorType,

errorMessage: errorMessage,

context: context

};


details.textContent = JSON.stringify(crashLog, null, 2);

modal.classList.remove('hidden');

modal.classList.add('flex');

};
